qgis-python in epel-7

This page displays detail informations of the qgis-python package. You might want go back to the main page of qgis-python.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2016-11-27 Dave Johansen - 2.14.9-1 - New upstream release
2016-06-07 Volker Froehlich - 2.14.3-3 - Version bump to be newer than F24
2016-06-06 Volker Froehlich - 2.14.3-2 - Move grass version to BR. This will avoid building with a different version than intended. The sub-package dependencies is taken care of by soname versions.
2016-05-23 Volker Froehlich - 2.14.3-1 - New upstream release
2016-04-20 Volker Froehlich - 2.14.1-2 - Change BR of qca to qca2 to make things easier in EPEL - Rebuild for BZ #1327360 - Make the requires on grass match an exact version again
2016-03-27 Volker Froehlich - 2.14.1-1 - New upstream release - Resolve the false sub-package dependency of python on server
2016-03-25 Devrim G端nd端z - 2.14.0-5 - Depend exclusively against GRASS => 7.0.3
